00695 
00696 # ifdef YYSTACK_ALLOC
00697    /* Pacify GCC's `empty if-body' warning.  */
00698 #  define YYSTACK_FREE(Ptr) do { /* empty */; } while (YYID (0))
00699 #  ifndef YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM
00700     /* The OS might guarantee only one guard page at the bottom of the stack,
00701        and a page size can be as small as 4096 bytes.  So we cannot safely
00702        invoke alloca (N) if N exceeds 4096.  Use a slightly smaller number
00703        to allow for a few compiler-allocated temporary stack slots.  */
00704 #   define YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM 4032 /* reasonable circa 2006 */
00705 #  endif
00706 # else
00707 #  define YYSTACK_ALLOC YYMALLOC
00708 #  define YYSTACK_FREE YYFREE
00709 #  ifndef YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM
00710 #   define YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM YYSIZE_MAXIMUM
00711 #  endif
00712 #  if (defined __cplusplus && ! defined EXIT_SUCCESS \
00713        && ! ((defined YYMALLOC || defined malloc) \
00714              && (defined YYFREE || defined free)))
00715 #   include <stdlib.h> /* INFRINGES ON USER NAME SPACE */
00716 #   ifndef EXIT_SUCCESS
00717 #    define EXIT_SUCCESS 0
00718 #   endif
00719 #  endif
00720 #  ifndef YYMALLOC
00721 #   define YYMALLOC malloc
00722 #   if ! defined malloc && ! defined EXIT_SUCCESS && (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
00723      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
00724 void *malloc (YYSIZE_T); /* INFRINGES ON USER NAME SPACE */
00725 #   endif
00726 #  endif
00727 #  ifndef YYFREE
00728 #   define YYFREE free
00729 #   if ! defined free && ! defined EXIT_SUCCESS && (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
00730      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
00731 void free (void *); /* INFRINGES ON USER NAME SPACE */
00732 #   endif
00733 #  endif
00734 # endif
00735 #endif /* ! defined yyoverflow || YYERROR_VERBOSE */
00736 
00737 
00738 #if (! defined yyoverflow \
00739      && (! defined __cplusplus \
00740          || (defined YYSTYPE_IS_TRIVIAL && YYSTYPE_IS_TRIVIAL)))
00741 
00742 /* A type that is properly aligned for any stack member.  */
00743 union yyalloc
00744 {
00745   yytype_int16 yyss_alloc;
00746   YYSTYPE yyvs_alloc;
00747 };
00748 
00749 /* The size of the maximum gap between one aligned stack and the next.  */
00750 # define YYSTACK_GAP_MAXIMUM (sizeof (union yyalloc) - 1)
00751 
00752 /* The size of an array large to enough to hold all stacks, each with
00753    N elements.  */
00754 # define YYSTACK_BYTES(N) \
00755      ((N) * (sizeof (yytype_int16) + sizeof (YYSTYPE)) \
00756       + YYSTACK_GAP_MAXIMUM)
00757 
00758 # define YYCOPY_NEEDED 1
00759 
00760 /* Relocate STACK from its old location to the new one.  The
00761    local variables YYSIZE and YYSTACKSIZE give the old and new number of
00762    elements in the stack, and YYPTR gives the new location of the
00763    stack.  Advance YYPTR to a properly aligned location for the next
00764    stack.  */
00765 # define YYSTACK_RELOCATE(Stack_alloc, Stack)                           \
00766     do                                                                  \
00767       {                                                                 \
00768         YYSIZE_T yynewbytes;                                            \
00769         YYCOPY (&yyptr->Stack_alloc, Stack, yysize);                    \
00770         Stack = &yyptr->Stack_alloc;                                    \
00771         yynewbytes = yystacksize * sizeof (*Stack) + YYSTACK_GAP_MAXIMUM; \
00772         yyptr += yynewbytes / sizeof (*yyptr);                          \
00773       }                                                                 \
00774     while (YYID (0))
00775 
00776 #endif
00777 
00778 #if defined YYCOPY_NEEDED && YYCOPY_NEEDED
00779 /* Copy COUNT objects from FROM to TO.  The source and destination do
00780    not overlap.  */
00781 # ifndef YYCOPY
00782 #  if defined __GNUC__ && 1 < __GNUC__
00783 #   define YYCOPY(To, From, Count) \
00784       __builtin_memcpy (To, From, (Count) * sizeof (*(From)))
00785 #  else
00786 #   define YYCOPY(To, From, Count)              \
00787       do                                        \
00788         {                                       \
00789           YYSIZE_T yyi;                         \
00790           for (yyi = 0; yyi < (Count); yyi++)   \
00791             (To)[yyi] = (From)[yyi];            \
00792         }                                       \
00793       while (YYID (0))
00794 #  endif
00795 # endif
00796 #endif /* !YYCOPY_NEEDED */
00797

02213      238,   238,   238,   238,   238,   238,   238,   238,   238,   238,
02214      238,   238,   238,   237,   237,   244,   245,     4,   245,   245,
02215      245,   245,   245,   245,   245,   245,   245,   246,   245,   246,

02240    Once GCC version 2 has supplanted version 1, this can go.  However,
02241    YYFAIL appears to be in use.  Nevertheless, it is formally deprecated
02242    in Bison 2.4.2's NEWS entry, where a plan to phase it out is
02243    discussed.  */

02247   /* This is here to suppress warnings from the GCC cpp's
02248      -Wunused-macros.  Normally we don't worry about that warning, but
02249      some users do, and we want to make it easy for users to remove

02255 #define YYBACKUP(Token, Value)                                  \
02256 do                                                              \
02257   if (yychar == YYEMPTY && yylen == 1)                          \
02258     {                                                           \
02259       yychar = (Token);                                         \
02260       yylval = (Value);                                         \
02261       YYPOPSTACK (1);                                           \
02262       goto yybackup;                                            \
02263     }                                                           \
02264   else                                                          \
02265     {                                                           \
02266       yyerror (YY_("syntax error: cannot back up")); \
02267       YYERROR;                                                  \
02268     }                                                           \
02269 while (YYID (0))

02276 /* YYLLOC_DEFAULT -- Set CURRENT to span from RHS[1] to RHS[N].
02277    If N is 0, then set CURRENT to the empty location which ends
02278    the previous symbol: RHS[0] (always defined).  */
02279 
02280 #define YYRHSLOC(Rhs, K) ((Rhs)[K])
02281 #ifndef YYLLOC_DEFAULT
02282 # define YYLLOC_DEFAULT(Current, Rhs, N)                                \
02283     do                                                                  \
02284       if (YYID (N))                                                    \
02285         {                                                               \
02286           (Current).first_line   = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 1).first_line;        \
02287           (Current).first_column = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 1).first_column;      \
02288           (Current).last_line    = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, N).last_line;         \
02289           (Current).last_column  = YYRHSLOC (Rhs, N).last_column;       \
02290         }                                                               \
02291       else                                                              \
02292         {                                                               \
02293           (Current).first_line   = (Current).last_line   =              \
02294             YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 0).last_line;                                \
02295           (Current).first_column = (Current).last_column =              \
02296             YYRHSLOC (Rhs, 0).last_column;                              \
02297         }                                                               \
02298     while (YYID (0))
02299 #endif

02458                        &(yyvsp[(yyi + 1) - (yynrhs)])
02459                                        );
02460       YYFPRINTF (stderr, "\n");
02461     }

02499 
02500 # ifndef yystrlen
02501 #  if defined __GLIBC__ && defined _STRING_H
02502 #   define yystrlen strlen
02503 #  else
02504 /* Return the length of YYSTR.  */
02505 #if (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
02506      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
02507 static YYSIZE_T
02508 yystrlen (const char *yystr)
02509 #else
02510 static YYSIZE_T
02511 yystrlen (yystr)
02512     const char *yystr;
02513 #endif
02514 {
02515   YYSIZE_T yylen;
02516   for (yylen = 0; yystr[yylen]; yylen++)
02517     continue;
02518   return yylen;
02519 }
02520 #  endif
02521 # endif
02522 
02523 # ifndef yystpcpy
02524 #  if defined __GLIBC__ && defined _STRING_H && defined _GNU_SOURCE
02525 #   define yystpcpy stpcpy
02526 #  else
02527 /* Copy YYSRC to YYDEST, returning the address of the terminating '\0' in
02528    YYDEST.  */
02529 #if (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
02530      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
02531 static char *
02532 yystpcpy (char *yydest, const char *yysrc)
02533 #else
02534 static char *
02535 yystpcpy (yydest, yysrc)
02536     char *yydest;
02537     const char *yysrc;
02538 #endif
02539 {
02540   char *yyd = yydest;
02541   const char *yys = yysrc;
02542 
02543   while ((*yyd++ = *yys++) != '\0')
02544     continue;
02545 
02546   return yyd - 1;
02547 }
02548 #  endif
02549 # endif
02550 
02551 # ifndef yytnamerr
02552 /* Copy to YYRES the contents of YYSTR after stripping away unnecessary
02553    quotes and backslashes, so that it's suitable for yyerror.  The
02554    heuristic is that double-quoting is unnecessary unless the string
02555    contains an apostrophe, a comma, or backslash (other than
02556    backslash-backslash).  YYSTR is taken from yytname.  If YYRES is
02557    null, do not copy; instead, return the length of what the result
02558    would have been.  */
02559 static YYSIZE_T
02560 yytnamerr (char *yyres, const char *yystr)
02561 {
02562   if (*yystr == '"')
02563     {
02564       YYSIZE_T yyn = 0;
02565       char const *yyp = yystr;
02566 
02567       for (;;)
02568         switch (*++yyp)
02569           {
02570           case '\'':
02571           case ',':
02572             goto do_not_strip_quotes;
02573 
02574           case '\\':
02575             if (*++yyp != '\\')
02576               goto do_not_strip_quotes;
02577             /* Fall through.  */
02578           default:
02579             if (yyres)
02580               yyres[yyn] = *yyp;
02581             yyn++;
02582             break;
02583 
02584           case '"':
02585             if (yyres)
02586               yyres[yyn] = '\0';
02587             return yyn;
02588           }
02589     do_not_strip_quotes: ;
02590     }
02591 
02592   if (! yyres)
02593     return yystrlen (yystr);
02594 
02595   return yystpcpy (yyres, yystr) - yyres;
02596 }
02597 # endif
02598 
02599 /* Copy into *YYMSG, which is of size *YYMSG_ALLOC, an error message
02600    about the unexpected token YYTOKEN for the state stack whose top is
02601    YYSSP.
02602 
02603    Return 0 if *YYMSG was successfully written.  Return 1 if *YYMSG is
02604    not large enough to hold the message.  In that case, also set
02605    *YYMSG_ALLOC to the required number of bytes.  Return 2 if the
02606    required number of bytes is too large to store.  */
02607 static int
02608 yysyntax_error (YYSIZE_T *yymsg_alloc, char **yymsg,
02609                 yytype_int16 *yyssp, int yytoken)
02610 {
02611   YYSIZE_T yysize0 = yytnamerr (0, yytname[yytoken]);
02612   YYSIZE_T yysize = yysize0;
02613   YYSIZE_T yysize1;
02614   enum { YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM = 5 };
02615   /* Internationalized format string. */
02616   const char *yyformat = 0;
02617   /* Arguments of yyformat. */
02618   char const *yyarg[YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM];
02619   /* Number of reported tokens (one for the "unexpected", one per
02620      "expected"). */
02621   int yycount = 0;
02622 
02623   /* There are many possibilities here to consider:
02624      - Assume YYFAIL is not used.  It's too flawed to consider.  See
02625        <http://lists.gnu.org/archive/html/bison-patches/2009-12/msg00024.html>
02626        for details.  YYERROR is fine as it does not invoke this
02627        function.
02628      - If this state is a consistent state with a default action, then
02629        the only way this function was invoked is if the default action
02630        is an error action.  In that case, don't check for expected
02631        tokens because there are none.
02632      - The only way there can be no lookahead present (in yychar) is if
02633        this state is a consistent state with a default action.  Thus,
02634        detecting the absence of a lookahead is sufficient to determine
02635        that there is no unexpected or expected token to report.  In that
02636        case, just report a simple "syntax error".
02637      - Don't assume there isn't a lookahead just because this state is a
02638        consistent state with a default action.  There might have been a
02639        previous inconsistent state, consistent state with a non-default
02640        action, or user semantic action that manipulated yychar.
02641      - Of course, the expected token list depends on states to have
02642        correct lookahead information, and it depends on the parser not
02643        to perform extra reductions after fetching a lookahead from the
02644        scanner and before detecting a syntax error.  Thus, state merging
02645        (from LALR or IELR) and default reductions corrupt the expected
02646        token list.  However, the list is correct for canonical LR with
02647        one exception: it will still contain any token that will not be
02648        accepted due to an error action in a later state.
02649   */
02650   if (yytoken != YYEMPTY)
02651     {
02652       int yyn = yypact[*yyssp];
02653       yyarg[yycount++] = yytname[yytoken];
02654       if (!yypact_value_is_default (yyn))
02655         {
02656           /* Start YYX at -YYN if negative to avoid negative indexes in
02657              YYCHECK.  In other words, skip the first -YYN actions for
02658              this state because they are default actions.  */
02659           int yyxbegin = yyn < 0 ? -yyn : 0;
02660           /* Stay within bounds of both yycheck and yytname.  */
02661           int yychecklim = YYLAST - yyn + 1;
02662           int yyxend = yychecklim < YYNTOKENS ? yychecklim : YYNTOKENS;
02663           int yyx;
02664 
02665           for (yyx = yyxbegin; yyx < yyxend; ++yyx)
02666             if (yycheck[yyx + yyn] == yyx && yyx != YYTERROR
02667                 && !yytable_value_is_error (yytable[yyx + yyn]))
02668               {
02669                 if (yycount == YYERROR_VERBOSE_ARGS_MAXIMUM)
02670                   {
02671                     yycount = 1;
02672                     yysize = yysize0;
02673                     break;
02674                   }
02675                 yyarg[yycount++] = yytname[yyx];
02676                 yysize1 = yysize + yytnamerr (0, yytname[yyx]);
02677                 if (! (yysize <= yysize1
02678                        && yysize1 <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM))
02679                   return 2;
02680                 yysize = yysize1;
02681               }
02682         }
02683     }
02684 
02685   switch (yycount)
02686     {
02687 # define YYCASE_(N, S)                      \
02688       case N:                               \
02689         yyformat = S;                       \
02690       break
02691       YYCASE_(0, YY_("syntax error"));
02692       YYCASE_(1, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s"));
02693       YYCASE_(2, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s"));
02694       YYCASE_(3, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s"));
02695       YYCASE_(4, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s"));
02696       YYCASE_(5, YY_("syntax error, unexpected %s, expecting %s or %s or %s or %s"));
02697 # undef YYCASE_
02698     }
02699 
02700   yysize1 = yysize + yystrlen (yyformat);
02701   if (! (yysize <= yysize1 && yysize1 <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM))
02702     return 2;
02703   yysize = yysize1;
02704 
02705   if (*yymsg_alloc < yysize)
02706     {
02707       *yymsg_alloc = 2 * yysize;
02708       if (! (yysize <= *yymsg_alloc
02709              && *yymsg_alloc <= YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM))
02710         *yymsg_alloc = YYSTACK_ALLOC_MAXIMUM;
02711       return 1;
02712     }
02713 
02714   /* Avoid sprintf, as that infringes on the user's name space.
02715      Don't have undefined behavior even if the translation
02716      produced a string with the wrong number of "%s"s.  */
02717   {
02718     char *yyp = *yymsg;
02719     int yyi = 0;
02720     while ((*yyp = *yyformat) != '\0')
02721       if (*yyp == '%' && yyformat[1] == 's' && yyi < yycount)
02722         {
02723           yyp += yytnamerr (yyp, yyarg[yyi++]);
02724           yyformat += 2;
02725         }
02726       else
02727         {
02728           yyp++;
02729           yyformat++;
02730         }
02731   }
02732   return 0;
02733 }
02734 #endif /* YYERROR_VERBOSE */
02735 
02736 /*-----------------------------------------------.
02737 | Release the memory associated to this symbol.  |
02738 `-----------------------------------------------*/
02739 
02740 /*ARGSUSED*/
02741 #if (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
02742      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
02743 static void
02744 yydestruct (const char *yymsg, int yytype, YYSTYPE *yyvaluep)
02745 #else
02746 static void
02747 yydestruct (yymsg, yytype, yyvaluep)
02748     const char *yymsg;
02749     int yytype;
02750     YYSTYPE *yyvaluep;
02751 #endif
02752 {
02753   YYUSE (yyvaluep);
02754 
02755   if (!yymsg)
02756     yymsg = "Deleting";
02757   YY_SYMBOL_PRINT (yymsg, yytype, yyvaluep, yylocationp);
02758 
02759   switch (yytype)
02760     {
02761 
02762       default:
02763         break;
02764     }
02765 }

02769 #ifdef YYPARSE_PARAM

02771 int yyparse (void *YYPARSE_PARAM);
02772 #else
02773 int yyparse ();
02774 #endif
02775 #else /* ! YYPARSE_PARAM */
02776 #if defined __STDC__ || defined __cplusplus
02777 int yyparse (void);
02778 #else
02779 int yyparse ();
02780 #endif
02781 #endif /* ! YYPARSE_PARAM */
02782 
02783 
02784 /* The lookahead symbol.  */
02785 int yychar;
02786 
02787 /* The semantic value of the lookahead symbol.  */
02788 YYSTYPE yylval;
02789 
02790 /* Number of syntax errors so far.  */
02791 int yynerrs;
02792 
02793 
02794 /*----------.
02795 | yyparse.  |
02796 `----------*/
02797 
02798 #ifdef YYPARSE_PARAM
02799 #if (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
02800      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
02801 int
02802 yyparse (void *YYPARSE_PARAM)
02803 #else
02804 int
02805 yyparse (YYPARSE_PARAM)
02806     void *YYPARSE_PARAM;
02807 #endif
02808 #else /* ! YYPARSE_PARAM */
02809 #if (defined __STDC__ || defined __C99__FUNC__ \
02810      || defined __cplusplus || defined _MSC_VER)
02811 int
02812 yyparse (void)
02813 #else
02814 int
02815 yyparse ()
02816 
02817 #endif
02818 #endif
02819 {
02820     int yystate;
02821     /* Number of tokens to shift before error messages enabled.  */
02822     int yyerrstatus;
02823 
02824     /* The stacks and their tools:
02825        `yyss': related to states.
02826        `yyvs': related to semantic values.
02827 
02828        Refer to the stacks thru separate pointers, to allow yyoverflow
02829        to reallocate them elsewhere.  */
02830 
02831     /* The state stack.  */
02832     yytype_int16 yyssa[YYINITDEPTH];
02833     yytype_int16 *yyss;
02834     yytype_int16 *yyssp;
02835 
02836     /* The semantic value stack.  */
02837     YYSTYPE yyvsa[YYINITDEPTH];

02879      The wasted elements are never initialized.  */

02893  yysetstate:

02896   if (yyss + yystacksize - 1 <= yyssp)

02900 
02901 #ifdef yyoverflow
02902       {
02903         /* Give user a chance to reallocate the stack.  Use copies of
02904            these so that the &'s don't force the real ones into
02905            memory.  */
02906         YYSTYPE *yyvs1 = yyvs;
02907         yytype_int16 *yyss1 = yyss;
02908 
02909         /* Each stack pointer address is followed by the size of the
02910            data in use in that stack, in bytes.  This used to be a
02911            conditional around just the two extra args, but that might
02912            be undefined if yyoverflow is a macro.  */
02913         yyoverflow (YY_("memory exhausted"),
02914                     &yyss1, yysize * sizeof (*yyssp),
02915                     &yyvs1, yysize * sizeof (*yyvsp),
02916                     &yystacksize);

02918         yyss = yyss1;
02919         yyvs = yyvs1;
02920       }
02921 #else /* no yyoverflow */
02922 # ifndef YYSTACK_RELOCATE
02923       goto yyexhaustedlab;
02924 # else
02925       /* Extend the stack our own way.  */
02926       if (YYMAXDEPTH <= yystacksize)
02927         goto yyexhaustedlab;
02928       yystacksize *= 2;
02929       if (YYMAXDEPTH < yystacksize)
02930         yystacksize = YYMAXDEPTH;
02931 
02932       {

02934         union yyalloc *yyptr =
02935           (union yyalloc *) YYSTACK_ALLOC (YYSTACK_BYTES (yystacksize));
02936         if (! yyptr)

02940 #  undef YYSTACK_RELOCATE

02943       }

02948       yyvsp = yyvs + yysize - 1;

06537   /* User semantic actions sometimes alter yychar, and that requires

06541      but that translation would be missed if the semantic action invokes

06587                                         yyssp, yytoken)
06588       {
06589         char const *yymsgp = YY_("syntax error");
06590         int yysyntax_error_status;
06591         yysyntax_error_status = YYSYNTAX_ERROR;
06592         if (yysyntax_error_status == 0)
06593           yymsgp = yymsg;
06594         else if (yysyntax_error_status == 1)
06595           {
06596             if (yymsg != yymsgbuf)
06597               YYSTACK_FREE (yymsg);
06598             yymsg = (char *) YYSTACK_ALLOC (yymsg_alloc);
06599             if (!yymsg)
06600               {
06601                 yymsg = yymsgbuf;
06602                 yymsg_alloc = sizeof yymsgbuf;
06603                 yysyntax_error_status = 2;
06604               }
06605             else
06606               {
06607                 yysyntax_error_status = YYSYNTAX_ERROR;
06608                 yymsgp = yymsg;
06609               }
06610           }
06611         yyerror (yymsgp);
06612         if (yysyntax_error_status == 2)
06613           goto yyexhaustedlab;
06614       }
06615 # undef YYSYNTAX_ERROR
06616 #endif
06617     }
06618 
06619

06621   if (yyerrstatus == 3)

06623       /* If just tried and failed to reuse lookahead token after an

06625 
06626       if (yychar <= YYEOF)
06627         {
06628           /* Return failure if at end of input.  */
06629           if (yychar == YYEOF)
06630             YYABORT;

06678             {

06717 yyabortlab:
06718   yyresult = 1;
06719   goto yyreturn;
06720 
06721 #if !defined(yyoverflow) || YYERROR_VERBOSE
06722 /*-------------------------------------------------.
06723 | yyexhaustedlab -- memory exhaustion comes here.  |
06724 `-------------------------------------------------*/
06725 yyexhaustedlab:
06726   yyerror (YY_("memory exhausted"));
06727   yyresult = 2;
06728   /* Fall through.  */
06729 #endif
06730 
06731 yyreturn:
06732   if (yychar != YYEMPTY)
06733     {
06734       /* Make sure we have latest lookahead translation.  See comments at
06735          user semantic actions for why this is necessary.  */
06736       yytoken = YYTRANSLATE (yychar);
06737       yydestruct ("Cleanup: discarding lookahead",
06738                   yytoken, &yylval);
06739     }
06740   /* Do not reclaim the symbols of the rule which action triggered
06741      this YYABORT or YYACCEPT.  */
06742   YYPOPSTACK (yylen);
06743   YY_STACK_PRINT (yyss, yyssp);
06744   while (yyssp != yyss)
06745     {
06746       yydestruct ("Cleanup: popping",
06747                   yystos[*yyssp], yyvsp);
06748       YYPOPSTACK (1);
06749     }
06750 #ifndef yyoverflow
06751   if (yyss != yyssa)
06752     YYSTACK_FREE (yyss);
06753 #endif
06754 #if YYERROR_VERBOSE
06755   if (yymsg != yymsgbuf)
06756     YYSTACK_FREE (yymsg);
06757 #endif
06758   /* Make sure YYID is used.  */
06759   return YYID (yyresult);
06760 }
